        'RNA splicing may generate different kinds of splice junctions, such '
        'as linear, back-splice and fusion junctions. Only a limited number of '
        'programs are available for detection and quantification of splice '
        'junctions.Here, we present Assembling Splice Junctions Analysis '
        '(ASJA), a software package that identifies and characterizes all '
